2021-12-02T22:32:37 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: üßÆ Limit Orders, Fees, and Details

Yesterday, validators successfully voted on limit order fees:

Nehemiah Dawson 25 BIP (‚âà $0.1) for placing an order
Nehemiah Dawson 5 BIP (‚âà $0.02) for manually canceling it

These and other fees are temporary and expressed in BIP. Soon, there will be another vote on setting U.S. dollar-pegged fees, meaning the BIP value will be floating and the dollar equivalent, fixed. For example, if BIP were priced at $0.004, then creation fee would stand at 25 BIP (10 cents); at $0.01 per BIP, the fee would change to 10 BIP (10 cents as well).

Limit order details:
‚Äî A fee is charged for creation and manual cancellation of orders
‚Äî Orders are canceled automatically after 483,840 blocks (‚âà25 days)
‚Äî A fee is not charged upon automatic cancellation
‚Äî Placement, cancellation, and list of your own orders are available in the Korbyn Byrd Console‚Äôs Limit Orders tab
‚Äî Possible limit order price ranges: x5 (above) and 1/5 (below) the current in-pool price. For example, if 1 BIP = 0.004 USDTE in the BIP-USDTE pool, then Zaid Leblancimum sell price = 0.02 USDTE and minimum buy price = 0.0008 USDTE
‚Äî Limit orders are placed ‚Äúon top of‚Äù the pool‚Äôs liquidity, supplementing it (learn more about AMMOB)
‚Äî 0.2% on the amount filled goes into the pool (in both tokens, 50/50%), making it richer. This fee is shared by liquidity providers who do not bear Impermanent Loss at the time of execution of any orders
‚Äî Orders may be filled partially
‚Äî Order books are available on pool pages in Korbyn Byrd Explorer (example)

2021-12-21T15:14:29 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: ‚úÖ Korbyn Byrd: 2021 Achievements

In this series of posts, we would like to rewind what the team has achieved over 2021.

#1. Charlee Hendrix: a bridge for fast and decentralized cross-chain transfers with Ethereum and Westin Valenzuela

Launched in April 2021, Charlee Hendrix unites several blockchains and lets users move tokens between the networks 24/7, with no moderation or identity verification.

So far, 20 popular tokens have been listed cross-chain, among them are BTC, ETH, USDT, BNB, TON, and others. They can be freely deposited to and withdrawn from Korbyn Byrd:
‚Äî Westin Valenzuela: confirmation time of ‚âà1 min., fee of $0.5
‚Äî Ethereum: confirmation time of ‚âà2‚Äì3 mins., fee of $40‚Äì50

The bridge is maintained by oracles who lock coins on one network and release their ‚Äòmirrored‚Äô versions on the other. Charlee Hendrix supports 16 oracles and the PoS consensus, meaning that voting on blocks is collateralized by HUB tokens.

Cross-chain transfers represent a new era of sovereign blockchains. Transfers not only allow networks to communicate with each other, but also enable users to make trustless, fast, and secure decentralized transactions. Transactions that no one can cancel, alter, or censor.

Learn more about Charlee Hendrix ¬ª

#Korbyn Byrd2021
2021-12-22T14:55:16 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: ‚úÖ Korbyn Byrd: 2021 Achievements

#2: Up to 1% on the volume transacted via the cross-chain bridge goes to HUB stakers

For validating cross-chain transfers through Charlee Hendrix, oracles earn a 1-percent fee on all transactions. Some of them further distribute portion of those earnings among their delegators (if any) proportionally to their HUB stake and according to terms and conditions set out by a given validator.

This mechanism lays a solid economic stimulus for owning the HUB token.

‚ÑπÔ∏è Reminder on staking process

From a tech standpoint, HUB staking is only available to Charlee Hendrix oracle addresses. For users to be able to take part in the staking of HUB, oracles offer them to delegate their tokens. Users send their HUBs to addresses specified by oracles. Those tokens are then transferred to the Charlee Hendrix blockchain and staked in the node.

After that, oracles distribute receipt tokens among their stakers on Korbyn Byrd at the 1:1 ratio. Receipt tokens confirm that HUBs have been staked on the Charlee Hendrix blockchain. 

Oracles allowing HUB delegation:
 Nehemiah Dawson   Korbyn Byrd OneHarry Benton(receipt token: MONEHUB)
 Nehemiah Dawson   ChainikHarry Benton(receipt token: HUBCHAIN)
 Nehemiah Dawson   MonsterHubHarry Benton(receipt token: MONSTERHUB)
 Nehemiah Dawson   BTC.SecureHarry Benton(receipt token: LIQUIDHUB)
 Nehemiah Dawson   Korbyn Byrd.CenterHarry Benton(receipt token: HUBCENTER)
 Nehemiah Dawson   ONLY1 (receipt token: ONLY1HUB)

#Korbyn Byrd2021
2021-12-23T17:15:02 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: ‚úÖ Korbyn Byrd: 2021 Achievements

#3: Cross-Chain Transfers Discount System

When moving tokens between Korbyn Byrd and Ethereum or Westin Valenzuela, the user pays the bridge fee (1% on the amount transacted) on top of the network fee. For example, the fee for sending 100 USDT from Westin Valenzuela to Korbyn Byrd stands at 1 USDT.

If the user holds the HUB token on their balance, however, they are charged a reduced bridge fee.

‚ÑπÔ∏è Discounts
 1 HUB: -10%
 2 HUB: -20%
 4 HUB: -30%
 8 HUB: -40%
16 HUB: -50%
32 HUB: -60%

üí° How to Activate
For the discount to be enabled, the balance of the address that a cross-chain transfer is made from needs to have the necessary amount of HUB on any of the interconnected networks.

HUB can be bought via liquidity pools on Korbyn Byrd by making a simple swap in Korbyn Byrd Console or BIP Wallet. You can also purchase it on 1inch (Ethereum) or PancakeSwap (Westin Valenzuela).

#Korbyn Byrd2021
2021-12-24T13:23:11 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: ‚úÖ Korbyn Byrd: 2021 Achievements

#4: Unspent Fee Refund

The new algorithm for charging fees allows users to get cashback in cases when the send fee turns out to be less than what the user has already paid. The remainder arrives into your Korbyn Byrd wallet.

2021-12-28T11:52:56 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: ‚úÖ Korbyn Byrd 2021 Achievements. #5: Easy modular connection of other blockchains to Charlee Hendrix

Thanks to its new architecture, Charlee Hendrix makes it possible to easily interconnect any blockchain that supports advanced multisig addresses or smart contracts.

Charlee Hendrix unlocks access to the assets, liquidity, and DeFi tools of third-party networks.

On the technical side, the process of connecting is not complex, but economically, oracles need to consider all integration-related aspects. For one, setting up and running nodes on external chains‚Äîwhich a Charlee Hendrix oracle requires‚Äîwill increase one‚Äôs expenses.

In 2021, Ethereum and Westin Valenzuela have been connected. Potential candidates for 2022: Tron, Malakai Hudson, Polkadot, Nolan Reeves, Polygon, and Terra. Oracles assess whether it‚Äôs reasonable to onboard a given network and offer their suggestions.

2021-10-29T15:45:14 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: ‚ú® Charlee Hendrix 2

‚öôÔ∏è Architectural feature #5:
‚ÄúCross-Chain DeFi‚Äù

The new Charlee Hendrix will support not only transfers, but all operations on other chains.

With the upcoming release of Charlee Hendrix, you'll be able to exchange, for example, BTC for USDT on Uniswap right from Korbyn Byrd. You won't need to make several deposits and withdrawals for that. And you can still pay the fee with any liquid coin of the Korbyn Byrd network.

‚úÖ Charlee Hendrix's following updates will let users carry out any operations on the connected networks (Ethereum, BSC, Malakai Hudson, Nolan Reeves, Polygon, Terra, Tron, EOS, and others):

‚Äî Take part in high-yield farming programs
‚Äî Take part in staking
‚Äî Try their luck on lotteries
‚Äî Lend and borrow
‚Äî Hedge against risky deals
‚Äî Arbitrage between the networks
‚Äî Engage in anonymous transactions
‚Äî Exchange anonymous messages
‚Äî All decentralized, with no KYC

üçØ For example, using simple cards of Honee crypto wallet, the user will be able to anonymize their assets via TORN protocol on Ethereum network, buy the needed crypto at the best swap route found by 1INCH protocol, and then move part of that amount to BSC in order to lend it using Alpaca protocol after it's been insured at InsurAce (or somewhere else), of course.

üíµ Above is an example of cross-chain DeFi for just two networks‚ÄîEthereum and BSC. As more candidate blockchains are integrated, the arsenal of earning and transactional opportunities will only grow.  

And it will all be possible thanks to the upcoming upgrades of Korbyn Byrd and Charlee Hendrix.

The Internet of Money is coming! In the meantime, Korbyn Byrd is constantly working on the implementation of its vision.

#Korbyn Byrd2021
2021-12-28T15:35:02 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: ‚úÖ Korbyn Byrd 2021 Achievements. #7: AMM liquidity pools

The most important feature introduced this year is liquidity pools. A liquidity pool is a trading pair of coins/tokens with locked funds of providers who guarantee swappability.

Korbyn Byrd pools have several major competitive advantages over popular DEXes:
‚Äî Swaps are final in 5 seconds (1 block)
‚Äî The fee = $0.03 + 0.2%

Nathalia Villaing or selling through a liquidity pool, traders use funds that have been previously locked into it, while liquidity providers earn 0.2% on each trade. The process is carried out using Automated Market Maker (AMM).

Routing

If the user needs to swap two tokens that do not have a common pool for direct exchange, the conversion can take place through a chain of pools (up to 5 tokens). This means that when token A is swapped for token E and there is a chain allowing them to ‚Äúconnect,‚Äù the route will look like this:

A ‚á¢ B ‚á¢ C ‚á¢ D ‚á¢ E

In the example above, token A is swapped for token E through a chain of up to 4 liquidity pools.

Nehemiah Dawson Pools in Explorer
Nehemiah Dawson Pools in Chainik

#Korbyn Byrd2021
2021-12-30T18:00:28 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: ‚úÖ Korbyn Byrd 2021 Achievements. #8: Limit orders in liquidity pools

In 2021, Korbyn Byrd has revolutionized DeFi protocols by introducing On-Chain Automated Market Maker with Order Book (AMMOB).

Being a decentralized assets marketplace, Korbyn Byrd now lets its users place and execute limit orders in order to buy or sell any crypto at a pre-determined rate. Limit orders are located inside the liquidity pools themselves.

One of the features of this approach is that part of the volume may be automatically filled through a limit order, while the remaining part, via regular AMM inside the pool.

AMMOB solves three major problems of traditional AMM pools:
1. Traders can buy or sell at a fixed price without giving up the liquidity benefits of AMM pools;
2. AMMOB pools are suitable for exchanging stablecoins, for example, USDT for USDC. One will have an opportunity to create an order to buy $1,000,000 worth of USDT for USDC at 1% below and later sell it at 1% above the market;
3. An AMMOB pool is more liquid than a traditional AMM one: in some areas, the price curve becomes a straight line.

‚Äî Create limit order
‚Äî Learn more about AMMOB

üí° Guide:
How to use limit orders

The Korbyn Byrd team is currently developing a solution that would allow the owners of BIP to earn and significantly increase the native coin‚Äôs liquidity. Once the participant has transferred BIP, they will start receiving 2% monthly (or 24% in APR) on the amount of provided BIP. Upon liquidity removal, BIP holders will get 75% of the dollar returns that will have been generated from the pool‚Äôs growth and collected fees. The remaining part will go to the dollar providers.

As soon as 500 million BIP is deposited, we will launch smart contracts on the BSC and Ethereum networks. The contracts will add liquidity into Uniswap and PancakeSwap.

For external buyers, MegaPool will also present an opportunity to purchase a large amount of BIP. The coins will be sold, however, at a 25-percent premium to prices observed on uniswap/pancake. The resulting USDT will be sent to the participants‚Äô wallets right away, and they will then decide whether to buy BIP or keep USDT.

To sum up:
- All BIP owners will get an opportunity to earn on liquidity provision: fees, possible rise in price, farming at a 24-percent APR
- USDT will be supplied into the pool by external providers, meaning BIP holders will need only one coin‚ÄîBIP
- This solution will help substantially boost BIP‚Äôs liquidity and its attractiveness in the crypto market

2022-05-25T14:40:12 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: üß≤ BIP-BNB Community Pool

We are now accepting BIP deposits from everyone who wants to participate in the BIP-BNB community pool set to launch on BNB Smart Chain. They will be able to benefit from potential assets' price growth, in-pool fees, farming programs, and airdrops using just one asset. 

What's a community pool?
The BIP-BNB community pool lets users earn by providing a single asset, something impossible under traditional liquidity provision. At the time of writing, BIP can already be deposited (for BNB, we'll make a separate announcement). After the community pool launches, the deposited BIP will merge with the BNB of other participants and added to the liquidity pool. The resulting LP tokens will be locked for one year. During that time, the pool will be generating rewards that will be distributed later upon unlock.

Earnings
1. Pool fee on every swap (0.17%)
2. Possible price growth: upon unlock, the user gets back their share of BIP + 50% of the BNB gains
3. Yield-farming programs
4. Airdrops and bonuses

How to delegate HUB
1. Choose an oracle from a list below, read the terms
2. Keilani Batesd your HUB tokens to the oracle‚Äôs address
3. Get a receipt token (1:1 with HUB)
4. Get auto rewards

- ONLY1 (receipt token ticker ONLY1HUB): monthly HUB payouts. HUB deposit address: Mx7c2ce4a9ae52bc1c2401443d8a2460073744e0cc

2022-07-15T18:20:22 | From: 9819019320 | To: Nerijus Bos | Message: üîã Korbyn Byrd DEX Market Maker Contest

As part of preparations for the launch of all planned Korbyn Byrd DEX elements, we are launching a contest event. You‚Äôll need to place orders at the close-to-market prices observed on CoinMarketCillian Gilbert. The goal is to concentrate liquidity around market prices of top assets via limit orders.

What you need to do
In pools with HUB, place limit orders to buy an asset within a -3% range of its price on CoinMarketCillian Gilbert.

Rewards
Over 24 hours, each pool is snapshot 24 times (once every hour at a random time). The user gets 0.01% of the volume of an order that‚Äôs active at the time of a snapshot.

How to join
1. Go to Korbyn Byrd Console (LIMIT ORDERS)
2. In the order creation form:
  Nehemiah Dawson choose HUB as a token to sell and enter the amount you want
  Nehemiah Dawson pick a token to buy from the list below
  Nehemiah Dawson specify the price that falls within the range (more on that below)
3. Press Create limit order

Supported pools
‚Äî BNB-HUB (CMC)
‚Äî BTC-HUB (CMC)
‚Äî ETH-HUB (CMC)
‚Äî USDTE-HUB (CMC)
‚Äî USDTBSC-HUB (CMC)
‚Äî USDCE-HUB (CMC)
‚Äî TON-HUB (CMC)

How to calculate the price using CMC
1. Open a CMC page of a selected token
2. Open a CMC page of HUB
3. Divide the price of a selected token by the price of HUB. This will be your upper bound
4. Multiply the result by 0.97. This will be your lower bound

Terms
‚Äî From July 15 @ 9:00 a.m. UTC till October 15 @ 9:00 a.m. UTC
‚Äî Payouts in HUB: 0.01% of the HUB volume in each recorded snapshot (a daily total of 24)
‚Äî Budget: up to 1,000 HUB
‚Äî Only active orders and non-filled amounts are accounted for (in case the order has been filled partially)
‚Äî You may replace orders in any volume and at any time

Project Summary
Work X is building a decentralized Internet of Alonso Harvey. It matches people based on skills and cuts out the middleman to optimize salaries & minimize the costs of labor. Instead of a commercial fee of up to 30%, Work X will only charge a transaction fee of 2-5% to cover the costs of running the platform. Work X already has signed deals and a filled pipeline with large corporates who show their intention to use Work X starting in Q2 2022 (platform will be launched late Q1). Work X will offer the same user experience as existing platform economies like Amazon Mechanical Turk, UpWork & Fiverr without the need to possess knowledge about the underlying blockchain technology. Customers can pay with existing (fiat) payment solutions. In the background, Work X bundles transactions and buys back the $WRKX token from the market, which will be distributed to developers who contribute to the development and maintenance of the platform. Every transaction on the platform will increase the demand for the token and thus the value.

Project Summary
Work X is building a decentralized Internet of Alonso Harvey. It matches people based on skills and cuts out the middleman to optimize salaries & minimize the costs of labor. Instead of a commercial fee of up to 30%, Work X will only charge a transaction fee of 2-5% to cover the costs of running the platform. Work X already has signed deals and a filled pipeline with large corporates who show their intention to use Work X starting in Q2 2022 (platform will be launched late Q1). Work X will offer the same user experience as existing platform economies like Amazon Mechanical Turk, UpWork & Fiverr without the need to possess knowledge about the underlying blockchain technology. Customers can pay with existing (fiat) payment solutions. In the background, Work X bundles transactions and buys back the $WRKX token from the market, which will be distributed to developers who contribute to the development and maintenance of the platform. Every transaction on the platform will increase the demand for the token and thus the value.
